<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stalknecht.html>stalknecht</a> (30911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stal.html>stal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knecht.html>knecht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">servant, employee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stallen.html>stallen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to park, put aside</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stalling.html>stalling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stalling.html>stallingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stalling.html>stallinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A place where gear can be stored, or where vehicles (especially bicycles) can be parked.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stamboom.html>stamboom</a> (15244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stam.html>stam</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trunk, <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a>; tribe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:genealogie.html>genealogie</a></span></li></ul>

***standbeeld.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:standbeeld.html>standbeeld</a> (8331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">stand</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beeld.html>beeld</a></i>, modelled on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statua</i>. Cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Standbild</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> of a <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> date.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">statue</span> <span class="defdate">[from 17th c.]</span></li></ol>

***stapel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stapel.html>stapel</a> (4659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapel.html>stapel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stapal</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stapulaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapel.html>stapel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapels.html>stapels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapeltje.html>stapeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pile</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">basis</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">foundation</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pedestal</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> trade</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">stockpile</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">stock</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">lutherie</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">sound post</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ziel.html>ziel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapel.html>stapel</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapel.html>stapel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapels.html>stapels</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cricket</span> (or alternatively, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:grasshopper.html>grasshopper</a></span>)
<ul><li><b>1597</b>, Karel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Mander, "Vijfd' Ecloga, oft Boer-liedt", <i>Bucolica <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Georgica, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, Ossen-stal <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Landt-werck</i>, page 30.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stapelen.html>stapelen</a> (19769)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapelen.html>stapelen</a></i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:stapelen.html>stapelen</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stappen.html>stappen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:stappen.html>stappen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:steppen.html>steppen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stapjaną</i>.

***stardust.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stardust.html>stardust</a> (55909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">star</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">dust</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stardust.html>stardust</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">stardusts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a powder with supposedly magic or charismatic qualities.
<dl><dd><i> My sister's <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> full of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stardust.html>stardust</a></b>, and she'd spend <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a> lazily planning her future life when she would make her big break in the movies. </i></dd></dl></li>
<li>A type of cosmic dust that condensed from cooling ejected gases from individual presolar stars and incorporated into the cloud from which the Solar System condensed.
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> are all made of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stardust.html>stardust</a></b>.</i></li>
<li><b>2004</b>, Ann N. Nguyen and <a href = vnd.unilang:ernst.html>Ernst</a> Zinner, "Discovery of Ancient Silicate <a href = vnd.unilang:stardust.html>Stardust</a> in a Meteorite", <i>Science</i>:
<dl><dd><i>Presolar grains <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> isolated in primitive meteorites only 15 years ago. These grains of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stardust.html>stardust</a></b> formed in the atmospheres of evolved stars and in nova and supernova ejecta.</i></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> astronomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A distant cluster of stars, resembling a cloud, the individual stars of which cannot be resolved.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">particles</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cosmic dust</span></li></ul>
</body>

***starfish.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a> (38889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">star</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fish</i>
<br clear="all" />
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Starfish.jpg/250px-Starfish.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="200" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Starfish.jpg/375px-Starfish.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Starfish.jpg/500px-Starfish.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="1024" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a></div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">starfishes</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of various <a href = vnd.unilang:asteroids.html>asteroids</a> or other echinoderms (not in fact fish) with usually five arms, many of which eat bivalves or corals by everting their stomach.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any many-armed or tentacled sea invertebrate, whether cnidarian, echinoderm, or cephalopod.
<ul><li><b>1755</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Erik_Pontoppidan" class="extiw" title="w:Erik Pontoppidan"><a href = vnd.unilang:erik.html>Erik</a> Pontoppidan</a>, trans. Isaac Kimbler, <i>Explanation of the Plate of Uncommon Star Fish, Extracted from the Natural History of Norway</i>
<dl><dd>But the largest of the <b>star-fish</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that sea <a href = vnd.unilang:monster.html>monster</a> called kruken, <a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:krabben.html>krabben</a>. [...] As this enormous sea-animal in all probability may be reckoned of the polype, or of the <b>star-fish</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a>, it seems that the parts which are seen <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> at its pleasure, and are called arms, are properly the tentacula, or feeding instruments, called horns as well as arms.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A woman who reluctantly <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> part in sexual intercourse, and lays on her back while spreading her limbs.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in translations of Japanese pornography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:anus.html>anus</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">chocolate <a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">various echinoderms</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">sea star</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">asteroid</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">inactive sexual partner</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">cold fish</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">dead fish</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">starfishes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">starfishing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">starfished</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To assume a splayed-out shape, like that of a <a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a>.
<ul><li><b>1981</b>, Kit <a href = vnd.unilang:reed.html>Reed</a>, <i>Magic Time</i> (page 229)
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> you damn bastard, why <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you let anybody love you," and then, before I could <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> her, she threw herself between us and the glowing suitcase, <b>starfishing</b> in the blaze of light as he <a href = vnd.unilang:blew.html>blew</a> up.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form into a splayed-out shape, like that of a <a href = vnd.unilang:starfish.html>starfish</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b>,  Polly Williams,  <cite>It Happened One Summer</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The sea roared up her nostrils, tunnelled into her ears, and flung her forward, then back, the current pulling her <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a> apart, <b>starfishing</b> her hands.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***starling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a> (27409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sterling</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sterlinge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">starlinc</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stærlinc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">stær</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">-linc, -ling</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sterlinck</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">starlings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A family, Sturnidae, of passerine <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>.
<ol><li>The common <a href = vnd.unilang:starling.html>starling</a>, <i>Sturnus <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> dark, iridescent plumage.</li></ol></li>
<li>A structure of pilings that protects the <a href = vnd.unilang:piers.html>piers</a> of a bridge.</li>
<li>A California fish, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/rock_trout" class="extiw" title="w:rock trout">rock trout</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Hexagrammos" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Hexagrammos"><i>Hexagrammos</i></a></span>, especially, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Hexagrammos_decagrammus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Hexagrammos decagrammus"><i>Hexagrammos decagrammus</i></a></span>, the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/boregat" class="extiw" title="w:boregat">boregat</a> or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bodieron" class="extiw" title="w:bodieron">bodieron</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***starre.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:starre.html>starre</a> (62886)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:starre.html>starre</a></strong>
</p>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">start</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">start</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:punt.html>punt</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***stasis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:stasis.html>stasis</a> (72723)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span></span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στάσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stásis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stead</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stasis.html>stasis</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stase.html>stases</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A slackening or arrest of the blood current, due not to a lessening of the heart’s beat, but to some abnormal resistance of the capillary walls.</li>
<li>Inactivity; a freezing, or state of motionlessness.
<dl><dd><i>His company <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> sized for growth, not <b><a href = vnd.unilang:stasis.html>stasis</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">science fiction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A technology allowing something to be artificially frozen in time, so that it does not age or change.</li>
<li>One of the sections of a cathisma or portion of the psalter.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">inactivity</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">stability</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">staticity</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">static</span></li></ul>
</body>

***statisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statisch</a> (33795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statisch</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statischer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:statisch.html>statisch</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">statischt</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>static, stationary, concerning a motionless state or object in equilibrium</li>
<li>concerning statics, statical</li>
<li>invariable, constant, immobile</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:statuut.html>statuut</a> (37724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">statute</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">statut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statūtum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***steed.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a> (33014)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">steda</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stallion, stud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">stoti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">herd of <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">stuot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">herd of <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stallion, especially in the sense of mount.
<dl><dd><i>The studded bridle on a ragged bough</i></dd>
<dd><i>Nimbly she fastens: <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>, how quick <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> love! <a href = vnd.unilang:--.html>--</a></i></dd>
<dd><i>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:steed.html>steed</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> stalled up, and <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> now</i></dd>
<dd><i>To tie the rider she begins to prove:</i></dd>
<dd><i>Backward she push'd him, as she would be thrust,</i></dd>
<dd><i>And govern'd him in strength, though not in <a href = vnd.unilang:lust.html>lust</a>.</i> — Shakespeare, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20140811201712/http://etext.virginia.edu/etcbin/ot2www-pubeng?specfile=%2Ftexts%2Fenglish%2Fmodeng%2Fpublicsearch%2Fmodengpub.o2w">"Venus and <a href = vnd.unilang:adonis.html>Adonis</a>".</a></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cycling<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bicycle.</li></ol>
</body> 
***steeds.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> (241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">stedes</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></i>, an adverbial genitive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:steden.html>stede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">steadfast, durable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> from the more common <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stade.html>stade</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stādi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stēdi-</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">stets</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>always, continually, all the time, every time, each time

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">steech</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:stijgen.html>stege</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">steyga</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*stega</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stairway</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*stigǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">staircase; <a href = vnd.unilang:ladder.html>ladder</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">stēge</i>, German <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:steg.html>Steg</a></i>.

***steekpenning.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:steekpenning.html>steekpenning</a> (55904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">steecpenninc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bribe, alm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steken.html>steken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:penning.html>penning</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steekpenning.html>steekpenning</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steekpenningen.html>steekpenningen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:steekpenning.html>steekpenninkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">bribe</span>, corrupt payment to buy an illegitimate favor (usually used in the plural form)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">steecspel</i>.
